9/29/19, 4:50 PM - Nischaya: def primeList(start,end):
    prime = [];
    for val in range(start, end + 1):
       if val > 1:
           for n in range(2, val): 
               if (val % n) == 0: 
                   break;
           else: 
               prime.append(val);
    return prime;


def mod(num):
    return -num if num<0 else num;


test = input();
for i in range(0,test):
    length = input();
    strIn = raw_input();
    strOut = "";
    
    for i in strIn:
        if(ord(i) in range(65,91)):
            prime = primeList(65,90);
            if(ord(i) in prime):
                strOut += i;
        
            else:
        
                for j in range(len(prime)-1):
                    if(ord(i)-prime[j]>0 and ord(i)-prime[j+1]<0):
        
                        if(mod(ord(i)-prime[j]) > mod(ord(i)-prime[j+1])):
                            strOut += chr(prime[j+1]);
                            break;
        
                        if(mod(ord(i)-prime[j]) <= mod(ord(i)-prime[j+1])):
                            strOut += chr(prime[j]);
                            break;
        
                    elif(ord(i)<prime[0]):
                        strOut += chr(prime[0]);
                        break;
        
                    elif(ord(i)>prime[len(prime)-1]):
                        strOut += chr(prime[len(prime)-1]);
                        break;
    
        elif(ord(i) in range(97,123)):
            prime = primeList(97,122);
            if(ord(i) in prime):
                strOut += i;
        
            else:
        
                for j in range(len(prime)-1):
                    if(ord(i)-prime[j]>0 and ord(i)-prime[j+1]<0):
        
                        if(mod(ord(i)-prime[j]) > mod(ord(i)-prime[j+1])):
                            strOut += chr(prime[j+1]);
                            break;
        
                        if(mod(ord(i)-prime[j]) <= mod(ord(i)-prime[j+1])):
                            strOut += chr(prime[j]);
                            break;
        
                    elif(ord(i)<prime[0]):
                        strOut += chr(prime[0]);
                        break;
        
                    elif(ord(i)>prime[len(prime)-1]):
                        strOut += chr(prime[len(prime)-1]);
                        break;
        elif(ord(i)<65):
            strOut += "C";
        elif(ord(i)>122):
            strOut += "q";
        else:
            strOut += "a" if 97-ord(i)<ord(i)-90 else "Y";
    print strOut;
